CREATE TABLE Category ( 
	CategoryID CHAR(5) CONSTRAINT pk_category PRIMARY KEY, 
	CategoryName VARCHAR2(50) NOT NULL, 
	CategoryDescription VARCHAR2(255) 
);

CREATE TABLE Delivery_Company ( 
	DeliveryCompanyID CHAR(5) CONSTRAINT pk_delivery_company PRIMARY KEY, 
	CompanyName VARCHAR2(100) NOT NULL, 
	CompanyPhone VARCHAR2(15), 
	BaseDeliveryCharge NUMBER(5, 2) DEFAULT 3.00, 
	CONSTRAINT chk_base_charge CHECK (BaseDeliveryCharge >= 0) 
); 

CREATE TABLE Member ( 
	MemberID CHAR(10) CONSTRAINT pk_member PRIMARY KEY, 
	MemberName VARCHAR2(100) NOT NULL, 
	MemberEmail VARCHAR2(100) UNIQUE NOT NULL, 
	MemberPhone VARCHAR2(15), 
	MemberBirthday DATE, 
	MemberAddress VARCHAR2(255), 
	MemberType VARCHAR2(10) DEFAULT 'Normal' NOT NULL, 
	MemberRegistrationDate DATE DEFAULT SYSDATE, 
	CONSTRAINT chk_member_type CHECK (MemberType IN ('Normal', 'VIP')) 
);

CREATE TABLE Voucher ( 
	VoucherID CHAR(5) CONSTRAINT pk_voucher PRIMARY KEY, 
	VoucherCode VARCHAR2(20) UNIQUE NOT NULL, 
	DiscountAmount NUMBER(5, 2) NOT NULL, 
	VoucherType VARCHAR2(20), 
	ExpirationDate DATE NOT NULL, 
	CONSTRAINT chk_discount CHECK (DiscountAmount > 0) 
);

CREATE TABLE Restaurant ( 
	RestaurantID CHAR(5) CONSTRAINT pk_restaurant PRIMARY KEY, 
	RestaurantName VARCHAR2(100) NOT NULL, 
	RestaurantPhone VARCHAR2(15), 
	RestaurantLocation VARCHAR2(255), 
	RestaurantType VARCHAR2(20), 
	CategoryID CHAR(5), 
CONSTRAINT fk_res_category FOREIGN KEY (CategoryID) REFERENCES Category(CategoryID), 
	CONSTRAINT chk_res_type CHECK (RestaurantType IN ('Halal', 'Non-Halal')) 
);

CREATE TABLE Member_Address ( 
	MemberAddressID CHAR(10) CONSTRAINT pk_member_addr PRIMARY KEY, 
	MemberID CHAR(10), 
	AddressLabel VARCHAR2(20), 
	UnitNumber VARCHAR2(20), 
	Street VARCHAR2(100), 
	City VARCHAR2(50), 
	State VARCHAR2(50), 
	Postcode CHAR(5), 
	IsDefault CHAR(1) DEFAULT 'N', 
	CONSTRAINT fk_addr_member FOREIGN KEY (MemberID) REFERENCES Member(MemberID), 
	CONSTRAINT chk_is_default CHECK (IsDefault IN ('Y', 'N')) 
);

CREATE TABLE Rider ( 
	RiderID CHAR(10) CONSTRAINT pk_rider PRIMARY KEY, 
	DeliveryCompanyID CHAR(5), 
	RiderName VARCHAR2(100) NOT NULL,
	RiderPhone VARCHAR2(15), 
	VehicleNumber VARCHAR2(15), 
	CONSTRAINT fk_rider_company FOREIGN KEY (DeliveryCompanyID) REFERENCES Delivery_Company(DeliveryCompanyID) 
);

CREATE TABLE Food_Beverage ( 
	ItemID CHAR(10) CONSTRAINT pk_food_bev PRIMARY KEY, 
	RestaurantID CHAR(5), 
	ItemName VARCHAR2(100) NOT NULL, 
	Price NUMBER(8, 2) NOT NULL, 
	CONSTRAINT fk_food_restaurant FOREIGN KEY (RestaurantID) REFERENCES Restaurant(RestaurantID), 
	CONSTRAINT chk_price CHECK (Price > 0) 
);

CREATE TABLE Group_Order ( 
	GroupOrderID CHAR(10) CONSTRAINT pk_group_order PRIMARY KEY, 
	MemberID CHAR(10), 
	RestaurantID CHAR(5), 
	CreationTime TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP, 
	CONSTRAINT fk_group_member FOREIGN KEY (MemberID) REFERENCES Member(MemberID), 
	CONSTRAINT fk_group_res FOREIGN KEY (RestaurantID) REFERENCES Restaurant(RestaurantID) 
);

CREATE TABLE Order ( 
	OrderID CHAR(10) CONSTRAINT pk_order PRIMARY KEY, 
	OrderVoucherID CHAR(10), 
	MemberID CHAR(10), 
	DeliveryCompanyID CHAR(5), 
	GroupOrderID CHAR(10), 
	OrderType VARCHAR2(20) NOT NULL, 
	TotalAmount NUMBER(10, 2) DEFAULT 0.00, 
	DeliveryCharge NUMBER(5, 2) DEFAULT 0.00, 
	OrderDate DATE DEFAULT SYSDATE, 
	CONSTRAINT fk_order_member FOREIGN KEY (MemberID) REFERENCES Member(MemberID), 
	CONSTRAINT fk_order_del_co FOREIGN KEY (DeliveryCompanyID) REFERENCES Delivery_Company(DeliveryCompanyID), 
	CONSTRAINT fk_order_group FOREIGN KEY (GroupOrderID) REFERENCES Group_Order(GroupOrderID), 
	CONSTRAINT chk_order_type CHECK (OrderType IN ('Pickup', 'Delivery')) 
);

CREATE TABLE Order_Voucher ( 
	OrderVoucherID CHAR(10) CONSTRAINT pk_order_voucher PRIMARY KEY, 
	VoucherID CHAR(5), 
	OrderID CHAR(10), 
	RedeemedAmount NUMBER(8, 2), 
	RedemptionTimestamp TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP, 
	CONSTRAINT fk_ov_voucher FOREIGN KEY (VoucherID) REFERENCES Voucher(VoucherID), 
	CONSTRAINT fk_ov_order FOREIGN KEY (OrderID) REFERENCES "Order"(OrderID) 
);

CREATE TABLE Group_Participant ( 
	GroupParticipantID CHAR(10) CONSTRAINT pk_group_part PRIMARY KEY, 
	MemberID CHAR(10), 
	GroupOrderID CHAR(10), 
	RestaurantID CHAR(5), 
	JoinTime TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP, 
	CONSTRAINT fk_part_member FOREIGN KEY (MemberID) REFERENCES Member(MemberID), 
	CONSTRAINT fk_part_group FOREIGN KEY (GroupOrderID) REFERENCES Group_Order(GroupOrderID), 
	CONSTRAINT fk_part_res FOREIGN KEY (RestaurantID) REFERENCES Restaurant(RestaurantID) 
);

CREATE TABLE OrderDetails ( 
	OrderDetailsID CHAR(10) CONSTRAINT pk_order_details PRIMARY KEY, 
	OrderID CHAR(10), 
	ItemID CHAR(10), 
	GroupParticipantID CHAR(10), 
	Quantity NUMBER(3) DEFAULT 1, 
	Subtotal NUMBER(10, 2), 
	CONSTRAINT fk_det_order FOREIGN KEY (OrderID) REFERENCES "Order"(OrderID), 
	CONSTRAINT fk_det_item FOREIGN KEY (ItemID) REFERENCES Food_Beverage(ItemID), 
	CONSTRAINT fk_det_part FOREIGN KEY (GroupParticipantID) REFERENCES Group_Participant(GroupParticipantID), 
	CONSTRAINT chk_qty CHECK (Quantity > 0) 
);

CREATE TABLE Delivery ( 
	DeliveryID CHAR(10) CONSTRAINT pk_delivery PRIMARY KEY, 
	OrderID CHAR(10), 
	DeliveryCompanyID CHAR(5), 
	RiderID CHAR(10), 
	DeliveryStatus VARCHAR2(20), 
	DeliveryEstimated TIMESTAMP, 
	ActuallyDeliveryTime TIMESTAMP, 
	CONSTRAINT fk_del_order FOREIGN KEY (OrderID) REFERENCES "Order"(OrderID), 
	CONSTRAINT fk_del_company FOREIGN KEY (DeliveryCompanyID) REFERENCES Delivery_Company(DeliveryCompanyID), 
	CONSTRAINT fk_del_rider FOREIGN KEY (RiderID) REFERENCES Rider(RiderID) 
);

CREATE TABLE Payment ( 
	PaymentID CHAR(10) CONSTRAINT pk_payment PRIMARY KEY, 
	OrderID CHAR(10), 
	GroupParticipantID CHAR(10), 
	MemberID CHAR(10), 
	PaymentAmount NUMBER(10, 2) NOT NULL, 
	PaymentMethod VARCHAR2(20), 
	PaymentStatus VARCHAR2(20), 
	PaymentDateTime TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP, 
	CONSTRAINT fk_pay_order FOREIGN KEY (OrderID) REFERENCES "Order"(OrderID), 
	CONSTRAINT fk_pay_part FOREIGN KEY (GroupParticipantID) REFERENCES Group_Participant(GroupParticipantID), 
	CONSTRAINT fk_pay_member FOREIGN KEY (MemberID) REFERENCES Member(MemberID) 
);
